INSTALL:
	DLL Plugin Loader 1.0
	https://www.nexusmods.com/skyrimspecialedition/mods/10546
	Simple DLL plugins loader.
	How to install:
		1. Go to your Skyrim Special Edition root directory. This is the same folder where SkyrimSE.exe is, usually "C:\Program Files (x86)\Steam\steamapps\common\Skyrim Special Edition\"
		2. Rename "binkw64.dll" to "binkw64_.dll" <- now there's a _ at the end.
		3. Put the "binkw64.dll" from downloaded archive into the folder mentioned in step 1.
		4. If you did it correctly you should have two files in your folder now: "binkw64.dll" and "binkw64_.dll", that's all, you can start the game now.
	How to check if everything is working correctly:
		1. Go to where you installed "binkw64.dll" (SkyrimSE.exe folder)
		2. Create a new file if it does not exist called "binkw64.log", make sure the extension says "log" and not "txt"!
		3. Start game and then exit game, it's fine if you only entered to main menu, no need to load into any save game.
		4. Now open the "binkw64.log" file, it will say what plugins if any were checked and whether they loaded correctly.
		5. If the file is empty then no plugins were found! This could indicate a problem with permissions or the folder path "Data\DLLPlugins" does not exist.
	NOTE:  2023.06.04 - DO NOT INSTALL!!!  can cause ctds.  Engine Fixes skse64Preloader does it better
	
	SSE Fixes 3.1.5.97
	https://www.nexusmods.com/skyrimspecialedition/mods/10547?tab=files
	Fix for a bug in Skyrim Special Edition that causes low fps.
	- requires DLL Plugin Loader
	- There is a bug in game code where if you have more than a few dozen ESP or ESM plugins installed the game FPS will become much lower in some areas. The ESP or ESM file content does not matter at all they can be empty dummy plugins with no masters. This happens because there are at least 4 nested iteration loops the game does in every frame and the lowest loop iterates for each plugin installed, normally this wouldn't be an issue but this code runs on multiple threads and for each plugin it locks a mutex every time, this is very slow. It's not even really a bug, just bad implementation.
	
	Animation Limit Crash Fix SSE 0.3-beta
	https://www.nexusmods.com/skyrimspecialedition/mods/31146
	The patch fixes the crash on game loading when you install too many animations with FNIS. The one mentioned in the article by Fore.  May also give you increased fps and loading speed by skipping a redundant part of code. More technical information you can find in the Developers section below.
	Incompatibility - SSE Engine Fixes - the option AnimationLoadSignedCrash must be disabled in the EngineFixes.toml (EngineFixes.ini in old versions) file to make it work together with the patch.

	Smooth Combat non Combat Animation 1.6 Smooth  INSTALL
	https://www.nexusmods.com/skyrimspecialedition/mods/52145
	This is a mod that made the difference between idle animations in combat and non-combat situations even when holding a weapon.
	- In Skyrim, whenever you pull out a weapon, you are always ready to fight.
	- However, this mode separates the idle animation from combat and non-combat situations when the weapon is taken out.
	- when an enemy is detected and enters a battle situation, an idle animation for each weapon is displayed according to the battle situation.
	- If the enemy disappears or dies and becomes a non-combat situation, it switches back to the non-combat idle animation.
	- requires Disable Turn Animation
	- uses Nemesis "Turning Animation Won't Affect Upper Body" feature
	- overwrites animated armory
	- uses DAR

	First Person Animation Teleport Bug Fix 1.0 Monitor144Hz
	https://www.nexusmods.com/skyrimspecialedition/mods/92795
	Behavior patch that fixes a vanilla bug where starting certain interaction animations in first person teleports you to the start of the cell you were in. Clean, compatible, and lightweight.
	- When playing vanilla interaction animations while in first person, there is an annoying bug where the player gets teleported to the beginning of the cell point after their hand glitches out on the screen.
	- This mod fixes that teleport bug while ensuring the animations play as normal in third person, without any scripts or workarounds.
	- It simply just prevents the transitions from ever happening in the first place when the player is in 1st person view. It does not touch 3rd person animations at all, and it consists of a tiny Nemesis patch that should be compatible with every other behavior edit out there.
	- Highly recommended when using a mod like JaySerpa's Immersive Interactions, which uses a lot of interaction animations. 
	- Install: 1. Install mod. 2. Run Nemesis, tick patch for mod, update engine, launch. 3. Done!

	C.O.I.N. - Merchant Exchange 2.1.0
	https://www.nexusmods.com/skyrimspecialedition/mods/70644
	C.O.I.N. is a fantastic mod by TateTaylorOH and VictorF. This mod allows you to exchange your coins from C.O.I.N. at general goods merchants instead of auto converting the coins.
	- Updated merchant exchange to be compatible with C.O.I.N. 2.1.0+
	- DO NOT USE THIS VERSION WITH AN OLDER VERSION OF COIN
	- The concept of finding other coins besides Septims in dungeons is something that makes the world feel much more grounded and realistic.
	One of the neat features of C.O.I.N. is that it serves as a lite economy mod. Each coin has a different value relative to a Septim. C.O.I.N. achieves this by auto converting the coin you pick up into its worth of Septims. This is a really creative way to put a dent into the amount of gold you retrieve from dungeons.
	- However, there are many times I wish I could pick up and keep the coin itself. Particularly when playing a character that likes to collect artifacts or other items.
	- Therefore, this mod makes the following changes to C.O.I.N.
	- Ask general goods traders to exchange your alternative coins for gold. Picking up a coin will no longer auto convert it to Septims. 
	- If you have any of the coins on your character the option to exchange them will be available for selection. The merchant will take all of your selected coins, and give you the appropriate amount of Septims.
	- The appropriate amount of gold with be deducted from the vendor's available gold.
	- If the vendor does not have enough gold, they will only take the coins from you that they can afford.
	- esp file - needs to be eslified
	
	C.O.I.N. - Merchant Exchange 2.1 - with bruma+wyrmstooth patch - KZ eslified esp replacer 2023.06.04
	- NEW MOD - ESLIFIED ESP REPLACER

	College of Winterhold Entry Requirements 3.2
	https://www.nexusmods.com/skyrimspecialedition/mods/24749
	Adds customizable skill level requirements to join the College of Winterhold.
	- This mod adds requirements to joining the College of Winterhold. It is fully voiced because Bethesda planned to have requirements to join the College at one point and recorded lines for being rejected. Also, when Faralda tests your magical prowess, she will test you on your highest eligible skill instead of randomly selecting one of the schools of magic. Like in Vanilla, you can still bypass the test with persuasion, or by showing Faralda that you are Dragonborn. In fact, the latter option has been changed to be available as soon as you unlock shouts, instead of only after the point when the main quest prompts you to go to the College.
	- As Bethesda originally planned, joining the College requires an "Apprentice"-level magic perk. This mod also adds an alternative requirement so that simply having a skill level of 25 will substitute for having the perk. The specific skill level can be customized or disabled using the MCM.

	True Hunter - fewer animals per square meter 5.0
	https://www.nexusmods.com/skyrimspecialedition/mods/25628
	Reduces the number of leveled animals with customizable spawn chances. No more predators at every turn.
	- Adds more realism, interest and challenge to hunting and makes traveling less annoying by decreasing the number of animals. It's done by adding a chance of disabling for each animal on cell loading, the chances are set separately for predators, "prey" and "ambient creatures". It's not how things are supposed to work in this game, just a workaround for maximum compatibility.
	- This mod only affects leveled NPCs, which means that completely predefined animals (such as wolves near Riverwood) won't be affected. They are not included to minimize mod conflicts. I also excluded animals that are in some location, i.e. not just in wilderness.
	-  Default spawn chances (100% in vanilla):
		Predators - 12% (wolves, sabrecats, skeevers, bears, spiders, trolls, etc.)
		"Prey" - 45% (deer, goat)
		"Ambient creatures" -  20% (fox, rabbit)
	- I also changed the ratio between foxes and rabbits from 3:2 to 1:5.
	- The small chance is justified by a really lot of spawn points in the world. You can customize the chances with the optional MCM or via xEdit.
	- There are two versions of the mod: with and without a MCM. The MCM allows you to change the spawn chances (but they can be changed even in the No MCM version via global variables). The MCM settings are shared by all saved games if you have PapyrusUtil installed, but it's not required.
	- COMPATIBILITY
		Conflicts with other mods that edit LvlPredatorScript.
		Place True Hunter before Animallica and Seasonal Wildlife Distribution.
		Place True Hunter after Requiem.
		Compatible with unleveling mods, SkyTEST, Wild World, No Predators on roads, Certainly Less Annoying
		Wildlife Spawns - CLAWS, Dynamic Animal Variants, Predator Animals Randomized Spawning.
		Only because of possible conflicts in the leveled list with foxes and rabbits, place the plugin before all mods that add new animals, letting them to ovewrite this edit if necessary.
		It doesn't edit every spawn point but affects all at once by changing their "base", so it is compatible with everything that adds, moves or removes them.
		It only affects vanilla animal types so you need a patch if you want it to work with mods that don't use vanilla leveled lists to spawn their animals.
	
	Customizable Companions Questline Progression Requirements 1.1 by lilebonymace  INSTALL
	https://www.nexusmods.com/skyrimspecialedition/mods/78308
	Increases and allows to customize the number of radiant quests required for advancing in the Companions questline.
	- In vanilla you need to complete one radiant quest before you can start Proving Honor, one before The Silver Hand and two before Blood's Honor, making pauses in the questline. This mod allows you to increase the duration of the questline by increasing the number of radiant quests required for its progression.
	- This mod does the same thing as The Companions - Earn your stripes and More Radiant Quests for the Companions, but they require patches for aMidianBorn Skyforge Weapons/Content Addon/Armor Variants Lite and any other mods that edit the Take Up Arms quest record. Moreover, a separate patch needs to be made for each of the provided options. My mod doesn't any vanilla records or scripts and therefore is compatible with everything, and also doesn't limit you to a few options.
	- The installer includes presets matching the mentioned mods. If you're not satisfied with the presets, you can easily set the desired number of radiant quests required for each of the three quests in a .json file that comes with this mod (Data\SKSE\Plugins\StorageUtilData\CompanionsProgressionReqs.json). You can set any positive numbers.
	- This mod applies the values when you start a new game (or on the first game loading when installing midgame), i.e. changes in the json won't be applied if the mod is already loaded. If you really need to change them, you can probably deactivate the .esp, save game, and activate it again.
	COMPATIBILITY
		This mod doesn't edit any vanilla records and is compatible with everything. Load order doesn't matter.
		Not needed and won't work with At Your Own Pace - Companions since it includes the same feature.

	SunHelm Survival and needs - Settings Loader 1.2.0  MaskedRPGFan
	https://www.nexusmods.com/skyrimspecialedition/mods/78535
	Modified MCM for SunHelm Survival and needs by colinswrath. Saves settings as you change them as default profile settings, adds delay for loads settings on startup, imports settings from an existing save, so you don't have to spend time in MCM again with each game. No plugin.
	DL: SunHelm Survival and needs Alternate Start Mods - Settings Loader 1.2.0 16 mar 2023
		For SunHelm Survival and needs v.3.1.4
	- This is QoL type mod. Modifies MCM for SunHelm Survival and needs by colinswrath. Saves settings as you change them as default profile settings, adds delay for loads settings on startup, imports settings from an existing save, so you don't have to spend time in MCM again with each game. No plugin. 
	- Disclaimer: SunHelm has a built-in mechanism for loading defaults. However, to use it, you need to save the settings, close the game, find the saved profile and move it to the location: "Data/SunHelm/Config/Default/SunHelm.json", and so every time you want to change the default settings.
	- This mod adds some very important simplifications and improvements:
	- Automatically saves your settings when you close MCM as defaults, so you don't have to close Skyrim and move anything to the default settings location.
	- Moves the loading of settings from OnInit to OnConfigInit and adds a 10-second delay to their loading, so that settings are loaded correctly even with a lot of scripts running at the beginning of the game.
	- Imports settings from an existing save: just open MCM and close it.

	SkyUI - Ghost Item Bug Fix 1.0
	https://www.nexusmods.com/skyrimspecialedition/mods/49106
	Fixes the issue where SkyUI favourite groups may not equip correctly under certain circumstances, such as after upgrading items.
	- Summary: This is an updated Papyrus script that fixes the Ghost Item problem where you if you upgrade or drop (amongst other things) an item what was in a SkyUI favourite group, you can no longer equip similar items in that group using the group equip key.
	- Problem description: You will most likely encounter this error if you have added an item to multiple favourite groups and upgrade or drop the item without first removing it from the groups. When you later add another item to these groups and that item occupies the same equipment slot as the removed item (e.g. rings, head, body), the new item might not equip and any item that is currently equipped in that slot will unequip when you use the group equip key.
	- This occurs because a function that is meant to blacklist missing or changed items stops looking after it finds the first group with an item, leaving any other occurrences as ghost items that block that equipment slot when you try to use those groups.

	Roggvir's Execution Scene Fixes 2.0 lilebonymace
	https://www.nexusmods.com/skyrimspecialedition/mods/74652
	- Fixes some bugs in Roggvir's execution scene that mostly happen with mods:
	- After the scene people go away very slowly if your timescale is lower than vanilla. It happens because the times between each group of people going away are specified in game time (0.1 hour), so that what feels good on timescale 20 feels like something is broken on timescale 8. With this mod the waiting time is calculated based on your timescale, so that the real time passed is the same as with vanilla timescale (i haven't simply changed it to real time for compatibility reasons). I capped the waiting time at 0.025 game hours, since RegisterForUpdateGameTime() doesn't work on extremely low values, but i've heard that too low timescale causes issues anyway.
	- NPCs can interact with Roggvir's body after the scene (go up to the scene, look at Roggvir's body and kneel down touching him, say generic dead body comments). This seems to mostly happen with mods that change AI detection settings. I workarounded it by preventing detection of dead Roggvir using po3's Papyrus Extender.
	Compatibility:
		Conflicts with mods that edit the same vanilla script. Must not be overwritten, otherwise it won't work.
		Compatible with USSEP and Scene Tweak - Roggvir's Execution - Restored Dialogue.
		A version for About Roggvir... can be found in the optional files.
	
	Scene Tweak - Roggvir's Execution - Restored Dialogue 1.0 AndrealphusVIII
	https://www.nexusmods.com/skyrimspecialedition/mods/58837
	A small tweak which restores some dialogue to the Roggvir execution scene.

	Fixes a vanilla bug in Shroud Hearth Barrow that can cause a script to get stuck running in your save forever. No ESP.
	
	Geirmund's Hall Pull Chain 1.0 by Livelynightmare
	https://www.nexusmods.com/skyrimspecialedition/mods/80218
	So I was doing Forbidden Legend the other day. You know, get the Gaulder amulet, kill the three bosses, reforge it. Got to Geirmund's Hall, dropped into the dungeon, killed the boss, and...the door didn't open. The door is supposed to open when you kill the boss.
	Next step obviously: check UESP. And in the bug reports, lo and behold, it's a known issue that sometimes the door simply fails to trigger properly. So I added a pull chain connected to the door. Now I can't get stuck there anymore, and neither can you.
	
	Glowing Spider freeze Fix 1.0
	https://www.nexusmods.com/skyrimspecialedition/mods/79359
	Fix the game freeze brought to you by glowing spiders!
	
	Consistency Fix - Vampire Scouts Only Spawn at Night 1.0
	https://www.nexusmods.com/skyrimspecialedition/mods/78222
	Most world encounters involving vampires happen during the night (8pm - 5am). The scouts that attack you when you exit Fort Dawnguard are not one of them, for some reason. This tiny tweak makes vampires intelligent enough to only spawn in at night.

	FUS RO DON'T - PushActorAway Crash Prevention Script Tweak 1.0
	https://www.nexusmods.com/skyrimspecialedition/mods/57816
	If the game tries to throw an NPC with PushActorAway, but the NPC hasn't fully loaded in yet, the game will crash. This mod adds checks to two vanilla scripts to make sure the caster and target both have their 3D fully loaded before trying to use PushActorAway, which stops the NPC from being thrown if the game isn't ready and prevents the crash.
